[ToolCallResult(tool_name='code_interpreter', tool_kwargs={'code': 'import numpy as np\n\ndef calculate_revenue_growth(ebitda_initial, ebitda_margin, multiple, debt_ratio, cash_initial, cash_exit, multiple_exit, irr_target, years=5):\n    """Calculates the required annual revenue growth rate to achieve a target IRR.\n\n    Args:\n        ebitda_initial: Initial EBITDA.\n        ebitda_margin: EBITDA margin.\n        multiple: Exit multiple.\n        debt_ratio: Debt-to-equity ratio.\n        cash_initial: Initial cash.\n        cash_exit: Exit cash.\n        multiple_exit: Exit multiple.\n        irr_target: Target IRR.\n        years: Number of years.\n\n    Returns:\n        The required annual revenue growth rate.\n    """\n\n    # Initial revenue\n    revenue_initial = ebitda_initial / ebitda_margin\n\n    # Calculate initial equity value\n    equity_value_initial = revenue_initial * multiple\n\n    # Calculate debt\n    debt = equity_value_initial * debt_ratio\n\n    # Calculate initial enterprise value\n    enterprise_value_initial = equity_value_initial + debt\n\n    # Calculate cash flow (simplified)\n    def calculate_cash_flow(year):\n        return (ebitda_initial * (1 + growth_rate)**year) * (1 - tax_rate)\n\n    tax_rate = 0.4\n\n    # Binary search for growth rate\n    low = 0.0\n    high = 0.5\n    growth_rate = 0.0\n\n    for _ in range(100):\n        temp_growth_rate = (low + high) / 2\n        \n        # Calculate terminal value\n        ebitda_terminal = ebitda_initial * (1 + temp_growth_rate)**5\n        terminal_value = ebitda_terminal * multiple_exit\n\n        # Calculate present value of cash flows\n        pv_cash_flows = 0\n        discount_rate = 0.15  # Example discount rate (adjust as needed)\n        for year in range(1, 5):\n            pv_cash_flows += (ebitda_initial * (1 + temp_growth_rate)**year) * (1 - tax_rate) / (1 + discount_rate)**year\n        \n        # Initial revenue\n    revenue_initial = ebitda_initial / ebitda_margin\n\n    # Calculate initial equity value\n    equity_value_initial = revenue_initial * multiple\n\n    # Calculate debt\n    debt = equity_value_initial * debt_ratio\n\n    # Calculate initial enterprise value\n    enterprise_value_initial = equity_value_initial + debt\n\n    # Calculate cash flow (simplified)\n    def calculate_cash_flow(year):\n        return (ebitda_initial * (1 + growth_rate)**year) * (1 - tax_rate)\n\n    tax_rate = 0.4\n\n    # Binary search for growth rate\n    low = 0.0\n    high = 0.5\n    growth_rate = 0.0\n\n    for _ in range(100):\n        temp_growth_rate = (low + high) / 2\n        \n        # Calculate terminal value\n        ebitda_terminal = ebitda_initial * (1 + temp_growth_rate)**5\n        terminal_value = ebitda_terminal * multiple_exit\n\n        # Initial revenue\n    revenue_initial = ebitda_initial / ebitda_margin\n\n    # Calculate initial equity value\n    equity_value_initial = revenue_initial * multiple\n\n    # Calculate debt\n    debt = equity_value_initial * debt_ratio\n\n    # Calculate initial enterprise value\n    enterprise_value_initial = equity_value_initial + debt\n\n    # Binary search for growth rate\n    low = 0.0\n    high = 0.5\n    growth_rate = 0.0\n\n    for _ in range(100):\n        temp_growth_rate = (low + high) / 2\n        \n        # Calculate EBITDA for each year\n        ebitda_years = [ebitda_initial * (1 + temp_growth_rate)**year for year in range(years)]\n\n        # Calculate terminal value\n        ebitda_terminal = ebitda_initial * (1 + temp_growth_rate)**years\n        terminal_value = ebitda_terminal * multiple_exit\n\n        # Calculate present value of cash flows\n        pv_cash_flows = 0\n        discount_rate = 0.15  # Example discount rate (adjust as needed)\n        tax_rate = 0.4\n        for year in range(1, years):\n            pv_cash_flows += (ebitda_years[year] * (1 - tax_rate)) / (1 + discount_rate)**year\n        \n        # Calculate IRR\n        initial_investment = enterprise_value_initial - cash_initial\n        irr = np.irr([initial_investment] + [ebitda_years[i] * (1 - tax_rate) for i in range(years)] + [terminal_value / (1 + discount_rate)**years])\n\n        # [ToolCallResult(tool_name='code_interpreter', tool_kwargs={'code': 'import numpy as np\n\ndef estimate_cost_of_equity(pe_ratio, borrowing_rate, d_e_ratio):\n    """Estimates the cost of equity based on P/E, borrowing rate, and D/E ratio.\n\n    Args:\n        pe_ratio (float): The price-to-earnings ratio.\n        borrowing_rate (float): The company\'s borrowing rate.\n        d_e_ratio (float): The debt-to-equity ratio.\n\n    Returns:\n\n        float: The estimated cost of equity.\n    """\n    # Assume a risk-free rate of 3% (this can be adjusted based on current rates)\n    risk_free_rate = 0.03\n    # Estimate beta using the D/E ratio. Calculate IRR\n    # Use a simple iterative approach to find IRR\n    irr = 2.0  # Initial guess\n    npv = 0\n    for i in range(num_years):\n        npv += free_cash_flow[i] / (1 + irr)**i\n    npv += (enterprise_value[num_years - 1] - initial_investment) / (1 + irr)**num_years\n\n    # Iteratively refine IRR until NPV is close to zero\n    for _ in range(100):\n        npv = 0\n        for i in range(num_years):\n            npv += free_cash_flow[i] / (1 + irr)**i\n        npv += (enterprise_value[num_years - 1] - initial_investment) / (1 + irr)**num_years\n\n        if abs(npv) < 0.001:\n            break\n        if npv > 0:\n            irr -= 0.005\n        else:\n            irr += 0.005\n        if irr < -1:\n            irr = -1\n\n    print(f"Returning: ({moic}, {irr})")\n    return moic, irr\n\n# Given parameters\ninitial_revenue = 70\ninitial_ebitda = 14\nrevenue_growth = 0\nebida_margin = 0.2 # We don\'t have the number of shares, so we\'re going to simplify and assume the market values reflect the number of shares.\n    # Therefore, combined_market_cap = acquirer_market_cap + target_market_cap\n    # Combined EPS = combined_earnings / (combined_market_cap / combined_pe)\n\n    # Let\'s simplify and assume that the market cap is equal to the P/E ratio times the earnings.\n    # This means that the combined market cap is the sum of the two market caps.\n    combined_market_cap = (acquirer_pe * acquirer_earnings) + (target_pe * target_earnings)\n\n    # [ToolCallResult(tool_name='code_interpreter', tool_kwargs={'code': 'import numpy as np\n\ndef cash_flow_statement(revenue, expenses, interest_rate, debt_principal, tax_rate):\n    """Calculates the cash flow statement for a firm.\n\n    Args:\n        revenue: Total revenue.\n        expenses: Total operating expenses.\n        interest_rate: Interest rate on debt.\n        debt_principal: Principal amount of debt.\n        tax_rate: Corporate tax rate.\n\n    Returns:\n        A dictionary containing cash flow from operations, cash flow from investing, and cash flow from financing.\n    """\n\n    # Cash Flow from Operations\n    ebit = revenue - expenses\n    interest_expense = interest_rate * debt_principal\n    pretax_income = ebit - interest_expense\n    tax_expense = pretax_income * tax_rate\n    net_income = pretax_income - tax_expense\n\n    cfo = net_income + interest_expense + tax_expense # Adjustments for non-cash items and interest/taxes\n\n    # Cash Flow from Investing (simplified - assume no significant investing activities)\n    cfi = 0  # No significant investing activities assumed\n\n    # Cash Flow from Financing\n    cfi_financing = - (interest_rate * debt_principal) - debt_principal # Principal repayment + interest paid\n\n    return {\n        "CFO": cfo,\n        "CFI": cfi,\n        "CFF": cfi_financing\n    }\n\n\n# Firm A (60% equity, 40% debt)\ndebt_principal_a = 100\ninterest_rate_a = 0.05\nrevenue_a = 500\nexpenses_a = 300\ncorporate_tax_rate = 0.21\n\n# Firm B (100% equity)\ndebt_principal_b = 0  # No debt\nrevenue_b = 500\nexpenses_b = 300\n\n\ncash_flow_a = cash_flow_statement(revenue_a, expenses_a, 0.05, debt_principal_a, corporate_tax_rate)\ncash_flow_b = cash_flow_statement(revenue_b, expenses_b, 0.05, debt_principal_b, corporate_tax_rate)\n\nprint("Firm A Cash Flow:", cash_flow_a)\nprint("Firm B Cash Flow:", cash_flow_b)\n'}, tool_id='709ac8a7-0bb3-4c86-bdcd-72ebc3fb01e9', tool_output=ToolOutput(content='StdOut:\nb"Firm A Cash Flow: {\'CFO\': 200.0, \'CFI\': 0, \'CFF\': -105.0}\\nFirm B Cash Flow: {\'CFO\': 200.0, \'CFI\': 0, \'CFF\': -0.0}\\n"\nStdErr:\nb\'\'', tool_name='code_interpreter', raw_input={'args': (), 'kwargs': {'code': 'import numpy as np\n\ndef cash_flow_statement(revenue, expenses, interest_rate, debt_principal, tax_rate):\n    """Calculates the cash flow statement for a firm.\n\n    Args:\n        revenue: Total revenue.\n        expenses: Total operating expenses.\n        interest_rate: Interest rate on debt.\n        debt_principal: Principal amount of debt.\n        tax_rate: Corporate tax rate.\n\n    Returns:\n        A dictionary containing cash flow from operations, cash flow from investing, and cash flow from financing.\n    """\n\n    # Cash Flow from Operations\n    ebit = revenue - [ToolCallResult(tool_name='code_interpreter', tool_kwargs={'code': 'import numpy as np\n\ndef calculate_dcf(cash_flows, discount_rate):\n    """Calculates the discounted cash flow (DCF) of a series of cash flows.\n\n    Args:\n        cash_flows (list): A list of cash flows.\n        discount_rate (float): The discount rate.\n\n    Returns:\n        float: The DCF value.\n    """\n    discount_factors = [1 / (1 + discount_rate)**i for i in range(len(cash_flows))]\n    dcf = sum([cf * df for cf, df in zip(cash_flows, discount_factors)])\n    return dcf\n\n# Example cash flows (without depreciation)\ninitial_cash_flow = 1000\nfuture_cash_flows = [500, 500, 500, 500]\n\n# Discount rate\ndiscount_rate = 0.1\n\n# Calculate DCF with initial cash flows\ninitial_dcf = calculate_dcf([initial_cash_flow] + future_cash_flows, discount_rate)\n\n# Depreciation increase\ndepreciation_increase = 25\n\n# Adjust cash flows to account for depreciation\nadjusted_cash_flows = [initial_cash_flow - depreciation_increase] + [cf - depreciation_increase for cf in future_cash_flows]\n\n# Calculate DCF with adjusted cash flows\nadjusted_dcf = calculate_dcf(adjusted_cash_flows, discount_rate)\n\n# Print the difference\ndifference = adjusted_dcf - [ToolCallResult(tool_name='code_interpreter', tool_kwargs={'code': 'import numpy as np\n\ndef calculate_net_income_difference(operating_income, debt_interest_rate, tax_rate):\n  """Calculates the difference in net income between a firm with debt and an equity-only firm.\n\n  Args:\n    operating_income: The operating income of both firms.\n    debt_interest_rate: The interest rate on the debt for the firm with debt.\n    tax_rate: The corporate tax rate.\n\n  Returns:\n    The difference in net income (firm with debt - equity firm).\n  """\n  # Assume a debt amount that results in 40% debt financing for Firm X.  This is needed to keep the example concrete.\n  # Let\'s assume total assets = 100, then equity = 60, debt = 40.\n  # Interest expense = Debt * Interest Rate = 40 * interest_rate\n  interest_expense = 40 * interest_rate\n  \n  # Net income before tax for firm with debt = Operating Income - Interest Expense\n  net_income_before_tax_debt = operating_income - interest_expense\n\n  # Calculate net income after tax for firm with debt\n  net_income_after_tax_debt = net_income_before_tax_debt * (1 - tax_rate)\n\n  # Net income for the equity-only firm (no interest expense)\n  net_income_equity = operating_income * (1 - tax_rate)\n\n  # Difference in net income\n  net_income_difference = net_income_after_tax_debt - net_income_equity\n\n  return net_income_difference\n\n# Example values\noperating_income = 1000\ninterest_rate = 0.05\ncorporate_tax_rate = 0.25\n\ndifference = calculate_net_income_difference(operating_income, interest_rate, corporate_tax_rate)\nprint(f"The difference in net income is: {difference}")'}, tool_id='8036634f-ca75-4908-9946-b5bb0d7bbb8a', tool_output=ToolOutput(content="StdOut:\nb'The difference in net income is: -1.5\\n'\nStdErr:\nb''", tool_name='code_interpreter', raw_input={'args': (), 'kwargs': {'code': 'import numpy as np\n\ndef calculate_net_income_difference(operating_income, debt_interest_rate, tax_rate):\n  """Calculates the difference in net income between a firm with debt and an equity-only firm.\n\n  Args:\n    operating_income: The operating income of both firms.\n    debt_interest_rate: The interest rate on the debt for the firm with debt.\n    tax_rate: The corporate tax rate.\n\n  Returns:\n    The difference in net income (firm with debt - equity firm).\n  """\n  # Assume a debt amount that results in 40% debt financing for Firm X.
